Payment","deliveryMethod":"CC_SAMEDAY","deliveryMethodGeneric":"CC_SAMEDAY","deliveryTime":"The money should arrive between now and 2 working days depending on the bank's processing time.","savingsPercent":"0.025","rate":"1.2426096","currencyIso3Code":"USD"}}},
                $sendingCountry = $('#calculator-sendingCountry'),
                $sendingAmount = $('#calculator-sendingAmount'),
                $sendingCurrency = $('#calculator-sendingCurrency'),
                $receivingCurrency = $('#calculator-receivingCurrency'),
                $sendingCurrencyAmount = $('.sendingCurrencyAmount'),
                $receivingAmount = $('#calculator-receivingAmount');

        $('#calculator-sendingAmount, #calculator-receivingAmount').on('keyup keydown change', function (e) {
            var $self = $(this),
                    value = $self.val().replace(',', '.'),
                    rateData = rates[$sendingCountry.val()][$receivingCurrency.val()],
                    rate,
                    sendingAmount;

            if (rateData) {
                rate = new Rate(rateData);

                $self.val(value);
                value = parseFloat(value);

                switch ($(this).attr('id')) {
                    case 'calculator-sendingAmount':
                        $receivingAmount.val(Flaber.round(rate.calculate(value), 2));
                        break;
                    case 'calculator-receivingAmount':
                        $sendingAmount.val(Flaber.round(rate.revert(value), 2));
                        break;
                    default:
                    // Do nothing
                }

                sendingAmount = parseFloat($sendingAmount.val());
                $('.rate').text(rate.options['rate']);
                $('.fee').find('.amount').html(rate.calculateFee(sendingAmount));
                $('.saving').find('.amount').html(rate.calculateSavings(sendingAmount));
                $('.total').find('.amount').html(rate.calculateTotalCost(sendingAmount));
                $('.disclaimer').find('.method').html(rateData['deliveryMethodDisplayName']);

                if (!isNaN(sendingAmount)) {
                    var date = new Date();
                    date.setTime(date.getTime() + 5 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
                    $.cookie('sendingAmount', sendingAmount, {expires: date, path: '/'});
                }
            }
        });

        $receivingCurrency.on('change', function(e){
            $sendingAmount.change();
        });

        $sendingCountry.on('change', function (e) {
            var currencyCode,
                    currencyData,
                    sendingCurrencyOptions = {},
                    receivingCurrencyOptions = {},
                    $element;

            if($sendingCountry.val()) {
                currencyCode = sendingCountryCurrencyMap[$sendingCountry.val()];
                currencyData = currencySymbolMap[currencyCode];
                $('.event-currency-switch').hide();
                $.each(rates[$sendingCountry.val()], function (key, item) {
                    receivingCurrencyOptions[key] = currencySymbolMap[key];
                    $('.event-currency-' + key.toLowerCase()).show();
                });

                $receivingCurrency.html(
                    Flaber.formatCurrencyOptions(receivingCurrencyOptions)
                );
                if($receivingCurrency.data('customSelect')) {
                    $receivingCurrency.data('customSelect').refresh();
                }

                sendingCurrencyOptions[currencyCode] = currencyData;
                $sendingCurrency.html(
                    Flaber.formatCurrencyOptions(sendingCurrencyOptions)
                );
                if($sendingCurrency.data('customSelect')) {
                    $sendingCurrency.data('customSelect').refresh();
                }
                $sendingCurrencyAmount.each(function (index, element) {
                    $element = $(element);

                    $element.html($.vsprintf(
                        currencyData['format'],
                        [
                            '<span class="amount">' + $element.find('.amount').html() + ' </span>',
                            '<span class="symbol">' + currencyData['symbol'] + ' </span>'
                        ]
                    ));
                });

                $sendingAmount.change();
            }
        });

        $sendingCountry.change();
    });
</script>                    </div>

        $('#calculator-sendingCountry').on('change', function () {
            var value = $(this).val(),
                countryData,
                payerItems = [],
                items = [],
                normalized;

            $('.switch-delivery-method, .switch-payment-method').hide();
            if(value) {
                countryData = countryDataBySendingCountry[value];

                $.each(countryData['payers'], function (index, value) {
                    payerItems.push('.switch-payer-' + value.replace('_', '-').toLowerCase());
                });
                $.each(countryData['deliveryMethods'], function (index, value) {
                    items.push('.switch-delivery-method-' + deliveryMethods[value]['normalized']);
                });

                $.each(countryData['paymentMethods'], function (index, value) {
                    normalized = paymentMethods[value]['normalized'];
                    if (($.inArray(value, ["CREDITCARD","DEBITCARD"]) !== -1)
                        && ($.inArray("CREDITCARD", countryData['paymentMethods']) !== -1)
                        && ($.inArray("DEBITCARD", countryData['paymentMethods']) !== -1)
                    ) {
                        normalized = paymentMethods["DEBITCARD"]['normalized'] + '-' + paymentMethods["CREDITCARD"]['normalized'];
                    }

                    items.push('.switch-payment-method-' + normalized);
                });

                if (items.length) {
                    $(items.join(', ')).show();
                }

                $('.switch-payer').hide();
                var $payerLogos = $('.switch-payer-partner-logos');
                $payerLogos.hide();
                if (payerItems.length) {
                    var $payerItems = $(payerItems.join(', '));
                    $payerItems.show();
                    if($payerItems.length) {
                        $payerLogos.show();
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    });

                    <div class="large-12 columns show-for-print">
                        <a href="https://azimo.com/en/account/contacts" class="send-money right button hidden">Send Money</a>

            <script type="text/javascript">
                Dispatcher.register(function(){
                    var payoutLocations = {};
                    $(document).on('change', '#representative-name', function () {
                        var $button = $(this).parents('.pickup-locations').find('.send-money');
                        if ($(this).val()) {
                            $button.removeClass('hidden');
                        }
                        else
                            if (!$button.hasClass('hidden')) {
                                $button.addClass('hidden');
                            }
                    });
                    $(document).on('change', '#representative-city', function () {
                        var city = $(this).val(),
                                $representativeName = $('#representative-name'),
                                id = city + country + currency,
                                country = 50,
                                currency = null,
                                $button = $(this).parents('.pickup-locations').find('.send-money');

                        if(!$button.hasClass('hidden')) {
                            $button.addClass('hidden');
                        }

                        $representativeName.html('');
                        if (city) {
                            if (!payoutLocations[id]) {
                                $.ajax({
                                    url: "https:\/\/azimo.com\/en\/country\/payoutrepresentatives\/format\/json",
                                    data: {
                                        country: country,
                                        currency: currency,
                                        city: city
                                    },
                                    dataType: 'json',
                                    type: 'POST',
                                    success: function (response) {
                                        if (response.success) {
                                            var optionsCities = '<option value="">Choose</option>';

                                            if ((response.data.toString() === '[object Object]') && !$.isEmptyObject(response.data)) {
                                                $('#representative-name').parents('.field').first().show();

                                                $.each(response.data, function (code, name) {
                                                    optionsCities += '<option value="' + code + '">';
                                                    optionsCities += name;
                                                    optionsCities += '</option>';
                                                });
                                                $representativeName.html(optionsCities).val('');
                                                $representativeName.data('customSelect').refresh();
                                                payoutLocations[id] = optionsCities;
                                            }
                                            else {
                                                $('#representative-name').parents('.field').first().hide();
                                                $button.removeClass('hidden');
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                });
                            }
                            else {
                                $('#representative-name').html(payoutLocations[id]).val('').change();
                            }
                        }
                        else {
                            $('#representative-name').html('').val('').change();
                        }
                    });

                    $('#pick-up-map').hide();
                });
            </script>
                            </div></form>        </div>
    </div>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        Dispatcher.register(function () {
            var ctrl = {

    <h2 class="no-margin font-16-px pad-h-bottom">
        Your money transfer to Indonesia - what to do with the money saved.
    </h2>
    <p class="font-14-px">
        Your friends or family might be wondering what to do with the savings you’ve made thanks to sending money to Indonesia via Azimo. So, we thought we’d offer up some ideas. Let’s say you’ve saved £20. That’s a lot of rice! But although you might be tempted to spend your Azimo savings on something sensible, we think you should think about some of these fun suggestions instead before deciding where that £20 should go…<br/><br/>
 
Indonesia has a rich, ancient and diverse culture. So why not take the kids and a couple of their friends and celebrate this amazing culture with...Laser Tag! Your Azimo savings are more than enough to treat everyone to a few rounds running around in the dark blasting each other. Find out who’s the best shot, form teams, and celebrate your victories afterwards with a Bintang Bir (and Coke for the kids).<br/><br/>
 
Or maybe you really do prefer to keep things traditional. In which case, why not make sure your Azimo transfer reaches home in time for your family’s special day. Whether it’s Eidil Fitri, Christmas, Waicak or even maybe Nyepi if you’re from Bali, there are any number of gifts and delicious foods you could splash out on. Or you might decide that everyone deserves a break from the kitchen. In that case, your Azimo savings will cover a delicious meal at a local ‘Rumah Makan’ for you and the people who matter most to you.<br/><br/>
 
Give someone special a break with Azimo. Send money to Indonesia today!    </p>

    <script type="text/javascript">

    	Dispatcher.register(function(){
            Flaber.loader.hide('global');

            $('.custom-select').customSelect();

                        MBP.hideUrlBarOnLoad();
            MBP.startupImage();

            $(document).on('click', '.modal-ajax', function (e) {
                var $self = $(this),
                        modal,
                        name,
                        data;

                if (name = $self.data('reveal-id')) {
                    modal = $('#' + name);
                    data = "name=" + name;
                    if ($self.attr("data-request-params")) {
                        data += "&" + $self.attr("data-request-params");
                    }
                    if (!modal.length || ($self.data('reveal-cache') === false)) {
                        if (modal.length) {
                            modal.remove();
                        }
                        $.ajax({
                            url: "https://azimo.com/en/index/partial/format/json",
                            type: 'POST',
                            async: false,
                            data: data,
                            dataType: "json",
                            success: function (response) {
                                if (response.success) {
                                    if (response.redirect) {
                                        window.location.replace(response.redirect);
                                    }
                                    else {
                                        var $container = $(document.createElement('div')).attr({
                                            id: name,
                                            'class': 'reveal-modal default ' + ($self.data('reveal-class') ? $self.data('reveal-class') : 'small-full large-large')
                                        });
                                        var $response = $(response.html + '<a class="close-reveal-modal">×</a>');
                                        $container.appendTo("body");
                                        $response.appendTo($container);
                                        $response.find("input").trigger("keyup");
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    }
                }

                e.preventDefault();
            });

            $(document).on('submit', 'form', function (event) {
                if ((event.result !== false) && !(event.isDefaultPrevented()) && !$(event.target).is(':hidden')) {
                    var timeout = $(event.target).data('loader-timeout');
                    timeout = timeout !== undefined ? timeout : 2000;
                    setTimeout(function(){
                        Flaber.loader.show('global');
                    }, timeout);
                }
            });
            $(document).on('click', '.slow', function (event) {
                var timeout = $(event.target).data('loader-timeout');
                timeout = timeout !== undefined ? timeout : 2000;
                setTimeout(function () {
                    Flaber.loader.show('global');
                }, timeout);
            });
                        $(document).foundation();
            
            if (window.location.hash === "#register-modal") {
                $(".register-button").click();
            }
    	});
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        function TrustevAuthenticationHook(result)
        {
            var digitalSignature;
            var digitalSignatureTimestamp;
            var sessionId;
            var stage1 = '';

            if (result != null && result.profile != null)
            {
                if (result.profile.trustevId != null)
                {
                    stage1 += result.profile.trustevId.value;
                }

                if (result.profile.emailAddress != null && result.profile.emailAddress.value != "")
                {
                    if (stage1 != null) {
                        stage1 += ".";
                    }
                    stage1 += result.profile.emailAddress.value;
                }

                digitalSignature = result.profile.digitalSignature.value;
                digitalSignatureTimestamp = result.profile.digitalSignatureTimestamp.value;
            }
            else
            {
                digitalSignature = Trustev.DigitalSignature;
                digitalSignatureTimestamp = Trustev.Timestamp;
            }

            sessionId = Trustev.SessionId;

            $('#js-trustev-digital-signature-input, .js-trustev-digital-signature-input').val(digitalSignature);
            $('#js-trustev-digital-signature-timestamp-input, .js-trustev-digital-signature-timestamp-input').val(digitalSignatureTimestamp);
            $('#js-trustev-session-id-input, .js-trustev-session-id-input').val(sessionId);
            $('#js-trustev-stage1-input, .js-trustev-stage1-input').val(stage1);
        }
    </script>
